if (!is_file('plugins/viathinksoft/language/dede/messages.xml')) {
	warn('File has vanished! Will re-create it: plugins/viathinksoft/language/dede/messages.xml');
	writefile_3();
	if (!is_file('plugins/viathinksoft/language/dede/messages.xml')) {
		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): plugins/viathinksoft/language/dede/messages.xml');
	} else if (sha1_file('plugins/viathinksoft/language/dede/messages.xml') != '990c50a8db853784d6e8355fd495569df6c2c11f') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): plugins/viathinksoft/language/dede/messages.xml');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('plugins/viathinksoft/language/dede/messages.xml', 0644)) {
		warn('Could not change file permissions of plugins/viathinksoft/language/dede/messages.xml');
	}
} else {
	if (@sha1_file('plugins/viathinksoft/language/dede/messages.xml') !== '990c50a8db853784d6e8355fd495569df6c2c11f') {
		if (@sha1_file('plugins/viathinksoft/language/dede/messages.xml') !== '2f75482c6022f21a62a5e5486b63b1220252e90f') {
			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: plugins/viathinksoft/language/dede/messages.xml');
			$tmp = pathinfo('plugins/viathinksoft/language/dede/messages.xml');
			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('plugins/viathinksoft/language/dede/messages.xml')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('plugins/viathinksoft/language/dede/messages.xml', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_3();
		if (@sha1_file('plugins/viathinksoft/language/dede/messages.xml') !== '990c50a8db853784d6e8355fd495569df6c2c11f') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): plugins/viathinksoft/language/dede/messages.xml');
		}
	}
}

if (!is_file('setup/index.php')) {
	warn('File has vanished! Will re-create it: setup/index.php');
	writefile_4();
	if (!is_file('setup/index.php')) {
		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): setup/index.php');
	} else if (sha1_file('setup/index.php') != '877954973d98fc5f4d5c40bb4f9edac8c6931dff') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): setup/index.php');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('setup/index.php', 0644)) {
		warn('Could not change file permissions of setup/index.php');
	}
} else {
	if (@sha1_file('setup/index.php') !== '877954973d98fc5f4d5c40bb4f9edac8c6931dff') {
		if (@sha1_file('setup/index.php') !== 'a155e9a0993c5b2cc06153cff5a89b6a92dc3067') {
			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: setup/index.php');
			$tmp = pathinfo('setup/index.php');
			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('setup/index.php')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('setup/index.php', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_4();
		if (@sha1_file('setup/index.php') !== '877954973d98fc5f4d5c40bb4f9edac8c6931dff') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): setup/index.php');
		}
	}
}

		if (@sha1_file('vendor/composer/InstalledVersions.php') !== '8a902bc1f6db2f3e3f4fd62e24293c67df03a89e') {

		}
	}
}

	@fwrite($fp, base64_decode('R1BMLTIuMS1vbmx5ICAgICAgICAgIAp0d2JzL2Jvb3RzdHJhcCAgICAgICAgICAgICAgICAgIHY1LjEuMyAgICAgICAgICAgICAgTUlUICAgICAgICAgICAgICAgICAgICAKdHdlZWIvdGlueW1jZS1pMThuICAgICAgICAgICAgICAyLjAuMyAgICAgICAgICAgICAg'));
	@fwrite($fp, base64_decode('IE1JVCAgICAgICAgICAgICAgICAgICAgCnZha2F0YS9qc3RyZWUgICAgICAgICAgICAgICAgICAgMy4zLjEyICAgICAgICAgICAgICBNSVQgICAgICAgICAgICAgICAgICAgIAo='));
	@fclose($fp);
}
if (!is_file('vendor/licenses')) {
	warn('File has vanished! Will re-create it: vendor/licenses');
	writefile_8();
	if (!is_file('vendor/licenses')) {
		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): vendor/licenses');
	} else if (sha1_file('vendor/licenses') != '7f0a082577243c9a06a9fc582eca4645fd895764') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): vendor/licenses');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('vendor/licenses', 0644)) {
		warn('Could not change file permissions of vendor/licenses');
	}
} else {
	if (@sha1_file('vendor/licenses') !== '7f0a082577243c9a06a9fc582eca4645fd895764') {
		if (@sha1_file('vendor/licenses') !== 'b556f78407b27695435f2998bb68ec4269dd4442') {
			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: vendor/licenses');
			$tmp = pathinfo('vendor/licenses');
			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('vendor/licenses')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('vendor/licenses', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_8();
		if (@sha1_file('vendor/licenses') !== '7f0a082577243c9a06a9fc582eca4645fd895764') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): vendor/licenses');
		}
	}
}


file_put_contents('.version.php', "<?php // Revision 703\n");
if (trim(@file_get_contents('.version.php')) !== '<?php // Revision 703') err('Could not write to .version.php!');


echo 'DONE'; // This exact string will be compared in Update v3

@unlink(__FILE__);
if (is_file(__FILE__)) warn('Could not delete '.basename(__FILE__).'! Please delete it manually');
